[30;1m462 | [0m[35mA common practice of CLI applications, as they span out and get larger, is to split their[0m
[30;1m463 | [0m[35mlogic into multiple, pluggable *sub-applications* (or *sub-commands*). A classic example is version[0m
[30;1m464 | [0m[35mcontrol systems, such as `git <https://git-scm.com/>`_, where ``git`` is the *root* command,[0m
[30;1m465 | [0m[35munder which sub-commands such as ``commit`` or ``push`` are nested. Git even supports ``alias``-ing,[0m
[30;1m466 | [0m[35mwhich creates allows users to create custom sub-commands. Plumbum makes writing such applications[0m
[30;1m467 | [0m[35mreally easy.[0m

[30;1m448 | [0m[35m    Relative paths are the "delta" required to get from one path to another.[0m
[30;1m449 | [0m[35m    Note that relative path do not point at anything, and thus are not paths.[0m
[30;1m450 | [0m[35m    Therefore they are system agnostic (but closed under addition)[0m
[30;1m451 | [0m[35m    Paths are always absolute and point at "something", whether existent or not.[0m
[30;1m452 | [0m[35m[0m
